    var slideIndex = 1;
    showDivs(slideIndex);


    function plusDivs(n, page, details) {

        switch (page) {
            case 1:
                if (details == 'female') {
                    $('#femaleClick').addClass("active");
                    $('#maleClick').removeClass("active");
                    $('input[name="firstgender"]').attr('checked', true);
                }

                else if (details == 'male') {
                    $('#femaleClick').removeClass("active");
                    $('#maleClick').addClass("active");
                    $('input[name="firstgender"]').attr('checked', true);
                }

                else {
                    $('#maleClick').removeClass("active");
                    $('#femaleClick').removeClass("active");
                }

                $("#firstgender").valid();
                if ($("#firstgender").valid() == true) {
                    showDivs(slideIndex += n);
                }
                localStorage.setItem('firstgender', details);

                break;
            case 2:


                if (details == 'mumbai') {
                    $('#clickmumbai').addClass("active");
                    $('#clickchennai').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickbangalore').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickhyderabad').removeClass("active");
                    $('input[name="currentcity"]').attr('checked', true);
                    localStorage.setItem('currentcity', details);
                }

                else if (details == 'chennai') {
                    $('#clickmumbai').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickchennai').addClass("active");
                    $('#clickbangalore').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickhyderabad').removeClass("active");
                    $('input[name="currentcity"]').attr('checked', true);
                    localStorage.setItem('currentcity', details);
                }


                else if (details == 'banglore') {
                    $('#clickmumbai').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickchennai').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickbangalore').addClass("active");
                    $('#clickhyderabad').removeClass("active");
                    $('input[name="currentcity"]').attr('checked', true);
                    localStorage.setItem('currentcity', details);
                }

                else if (details == 'hyderabad') {
                    $('#clickmumbai').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickchennai').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickbangalore').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickhyderabad').addClass("active");
                    $('input[name="currentcity"]').attr('checked', true);
                    localStorage.setItem('currentcity', details);
                }

                else {
                    $('#clickmumbai').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickchennai').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickbangalore').removeClass("active");
                    $('#clickhyderabad').removeClass("active");
                    localStorage.setItem('currentcity', $("#city option:selected").val());
                }

                $("#currentcity").valid();
                if ($("#currentcity").valid() == true) {
                    showDivs(slideIndex += n);
                }
                break;
            case 3:

                $("#companyname").valid();
                if ($("#companyname").valid() == true) {
                    showDivs(slideIndex += n);
                }
                localStorage.setItem('companyname', $("#companyname").val());


                $("#namecompanyname").valid();
                if ($("#namecompanyname").valid() == true) {
                }
                localStorage.setItem('companytype', details);
                if (document.getElementById('clicksalarised').checked == true) {
                    localStorage.setItem('companytype', 'salaried');
                } else if (document.getElementById('clickselfemployed').checked == true) {
                    localStorage.setItem('companytype', 'self-employed');
                }

                break;
            case 4:
                $("#salaryamount").valid();
                if ($("#salaryamount").valid() == true) {
                    showDivs(slideIndex += n);
                }


                localStorage.setItem('salaryamount', $("#salaryamount").val());
                localStorage.setItem('salaryamount', $("#myTextBox").val());

                break;
            case 5:
                $("#residency").valid();
                if ($("#residency").valid() == true) {
                    showDivs(slideIndex += n);
                }

                localStorage.setItem('residency', details);
                break;

            case 6:

                $('#fgender').val(localStorage.getItem('firstgender'));
                $('#ccity').val(localStorage.getItem('currentcity'));
                $('#cname').val(localStorage.getItem('companyname'));
                $('#samount').val(localStorage.getItem('salaryamount'));
                $('#cresidency').val(localStorage.getItem('residency'));
                $('#eamount').val(localStorage.getItem('emiamount'));
                $('#ctype').val(localStorage.getItem('companytype'));

                var type = "subproductpage";
                var months = 10;
                localStorage.setItem('emiamount', $("#emiamount").val());
                localStorage.setItem('emiamount', $("#myTextBox2").val());


                var companylist = availableTags;
                var salaryamount = localStorage.getItem('salaryamount') - localStorage.getItem('emiamount');
                if (type == "productpage") {
                    if (salaryamount >= "50000") {
                        $('#message').text('You are just a click away from finding best offers!');

                        setTimeout(function () {
                            window.location.href = "https://banksdirect.in/";
                        }, 10000);

                    } else if (salaryamount <= "5000") {
                        $('#message').text('You are just a click away from finding best offers!');
                        setTimeout(function () {
                            window.location.href = "https://banksdirect.in/paisa-guru/";
                        }, 10000);
                    }
                    else if (salaryamount <= "8000") {
                        $('#message').text('You are just a click away from finding best offers!');
                    }
                } else if (type == "subproductpage") {

                    var companyname = localStorage.getItem('companyname');

                    var companyexist;

                    for (i = 0; i < availableTags.length; i++) {
                        if (companyname == availableTags[i]) {
                            companyexist = true;
                        }
                    }

                    if (salaryamount >= "20000" && companyexist == true) {
//                            $('#eligleAmount').text('Your maximum eligible amount is '+ salary * months);
                        $('#message').text('You are just a click away from finding best offers!');
                    } else {
                        $('#eligleAmount').text('You are just a click away from finding best offers!');

                        if (companyexist == false || companyexist == undefined) {
                            $('#message').text('You are just a click away from finding best offers!');
                        } else {
                            $('#message').text('You are just a click away from finding best offers!');
                        }
                    }
                }

                showDivs(slideIndex += n);

                break;

            case 7 :
//                $("#contactdetails").valid();
//                $("#contactdetails").valid();
                $(".cnt-det-name").valid();
                $(".cnt-det-mobno").valid();

                localStorage.setItem('Fullname', $(".cnt-det-name").val());
                localStorage.setItem('Mobilenumber', $(".cnt-det-mobno").val());


                if ($(".cnt-det-name").valid() == true && $(".cnt-det-mobno").valid() == true) {
                    var subject = "User details";
                    var formattedBody = "Gender : " + localStorage.getItem('firstgender') + "\n City : " + localStorage.getItem('currentcity') + "\n emiamount : " + localStorage.getItem('emiamount') + "\n Employ Type : " + localStorage.getItem('companytype') + "\n Company Name : " + localStorage.getItem('companyname') + "\n Residence : " + localStorage.getItem('residency') + "\n salaryamount : " + localStorage.getItem('salaryamount') + "\n Fullname : " + localStorage.getItem('Fullname') + "\n Mobilenumber : " + localStorage.getItem('Mobilenumber');

                }


                break;

            default:

        }
    }

    function showDivs(n) {
        var i;
        var x = document.getElementsByClassName("mySlides");
        if (n > x.length) {
            slideIndex = 1
        }
        if (n < 1) {
            slideIndex = x.length
        }
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
            x[i].style.display = "none";
        }
        x[slideIndex - 1].style.display = "block";
    }

<script>

    $("#myTextBox").on("change paste keyup", function () {
        $('.range-slider__range').val($(this).val());
//        $('#salaryamount').val($(this).val());
    });


    var rangeSlider = function () {
        var slider = $('.range-slider'),
                range = $('.range-slider__range'),
                value = $('.range-slider__value');

        slider.each(function () {

            value.each(function () {
                var value = $(this).prev().attr('value');
                $(this).html(value);
            });

            range.on('input', function () {
//                $(this).next(value).html(this.value);
//                $('.range-slider__value').html(this.value);
                $('.range-slider__value').val(this.value);
            });
        });
    };

    rangeSlider();
</script>

<script>


       $("#myTextBox3").on("change paste keyup", function () {
        $('.range-slider__range3').val($(this).val());
           $('.loanamount').html(this.value);
           $('.loanamount').val(this.value);
            });

    var rangeSlider = function () {
        var slider = $('.range-slider3'),
                range = $('.range-slider__range3'),
                value = $('.range-slider__value3');

        slider.each(function () {

            value.each(function () {
                var value = $(this).prev().attr('value');
                $(this).html(value);
            });

            range.on('input', function () {
                $(this).next(value).html(this.value);
                $('.loanamount').html(this.value);
                $('.loanamount').val(this.value);
            });


        });
    };

    rangeSlider();

       $("#myTextBox4").on("change paste keyup", function () {
           $('.range-slider__range4').val($(this).val());
           $('.loantenture').html(this.value);
           $('.loantenture').val(this.value);
       });



    var rangeSlider = function () {
        var slider = $('.range-slider4'),
                range = $('.range-slider__range4'),
//                range1 = $('.range-slider__range4'),
                value = $('.range-slider__value4');

        slider.each(function () {

            value.each(function () {
                var value = $(this).prev().attr('value');
                $(this).html(value);
            });

            range.on('input', function () {
                $(this).next(value).html(this.value);
                $('.loantenture').html(this.value);
                $('.loantenture').val(this.value);
            });

        });
    };

    rangeSlider();


    $('#interestrate').bind('input', function (value) {
//        if (value.target.value == "" || value.target.value == "%") {
//            value.target.value = "10.25%";
//        }
        if (value.target.value.slice(-1) == "%") {
            $('.loanpercent').text(value.target.value);
        } else {
            $('.loanpercent').text(value.target.value + '%');
        }
    });

    $('#processingfee').bind('input', function (value) {

//        if (value.target.value == "" || value.target.value == "%") {
//            value.target.value = "2%";
//        }
        if (value.target.value.slice(-1) == "%") {
            $('.processfee').text(value.target.value);
        } else {
            $('.processfee').text(value.target.value + '%');
        }
    });

    var totalloaninterest, procesingfeeamount;
    function calculateInterest() {


        var number = $('.range-slider__range4')[0].value;
        var splitstring = number.toString().split('.');
        var years = parseInt(splitstring[0]);
        var months = splitstring[1];
        var totalMonths = years * 12;

        if (months != undefined) {
            totalMonths = totalMonths + parseInt(months);
        } else {
            totalMonths = totalMonths;
        }

        var tenture = totalMonths;
        var loanAmount = $('.range-slider__range3')[0].value;

        var interestPer;
        var interestforcompound = $('#interestrate').val() || 10.25;
        if ($('#interestrate').val() == "") {
            interestPer = 10.25 / 12 / 100;
        } else {
            interestPer = $('#interestrate').val() / 12 / 100;
        }

        var procesingFee;

        if ($('#processingfee').val() == "") {
            procesingFee = 2;
        } else {
            procesingFee = $('#processingfee').val();
        }

        var totalamunt;
        totalamunt = Math.round(loanAmount) * interestPer / (1 - (Math.pow(1 / (1 + interestPer), tenture)));
        totalamunt = totalamunt.toFixed(2);

        procesingfeeamount = loanAmount / 100 * procesingFee;
        $('.processingamount').text(procesingfeeamount);
        $('.emiamount').text(Math.round(totalamunt));


        totalloaninterest = totalamunt * tenture - loanAmount;

        $('.interestamount').text(Math.round(totalloaninterest));

        var totalemiamount = parseInt(loanAmount) + totalloaninterest + procesingfeeamount;
        $('.totalemiamount').text(Math.round(totalemiamount));

        //computeSchedule(loanAmount, interestforcompound, 12, $('.range-slider__range4')[0].value, Math.round(totalloaninterest));

        var data = [{
            values: [$('.range-slider__range3')[0].value, Math.round(totalloaninterest), procesingfeeamount],
            labels: ['Loan Amount', 'Total Interest Due', 'Processing Fee'],
            type: 'pie'
        }];

        var layout = {
            height: 380,
            width: 480
        };

        Plotly.newPlot('myDiv', data, layout);

        commitData($('.range-slider__range3')[0].value, interestforcompound, tenture);
    }

    var data = [{
        values: [50000, 2819, 1000],
        labels: ['Loan Amount', 'Total Interest Due', 'Processing Fee'],
        type: 'pie'
    }];

    var layout = {
        height: 380,
        width: 480
    };
    Plotly.newPlot('myDiv', data, layout);

    commitData(50000, 10.25, 6);

    function commitData(loanAmount, roi, months) {
        // Declair and initialize the variables
        var eleId;
        var eleDat;
        var loanName = "james";
        var loanAmount = loanAmount;
        var intRate = roi;
        var numPay = months;
        var loopNum;
        var tagNum;
        var tagNam, tagNam1, tagNam2, tagNam3, tagNam4;
        // Render the display tables to echo the user input
        var document;
        document = $('#amortization').html('');
        // Render the amortization table, this table displays the number of
        // rows specified by the number of payments input by the user in the numPay field.
        var docline1 = document.append("<td id='pmtTabsty'><table border=" + "1" + " id='pmtTab'><tr style='background-color:white'><td id='numHead'>Payment Number</td><td id='pt'>Principal Paid</td><td id='oil'>Interest Paid</td><td id='til'>Total Payment</td><td id='newBal'>Outstanding Balance</td></tr>");
        for (var i = 1; i <= numPay; i++) {
            loopNum = i;
            tagNam = "n" + loopNum.toString(10);
            tagNam1 = "p" + loopNum.toString(10);
            tagNam2 = "oi" + loopNum.toString(10);
            tagNam3 = "ti" + loopNum.toString(10);
            tagNam4 = "nb" + loopNum.toString(10);
            $('#pmtTab').append("<tr style='background-color:white'><td id=tagNam>" + i + "</td><td id=" + tagNam1 + "></td><td id=" + tagNam2 + "></td><td id=" + tagNam3 + "></td><td id=" + tagNam4 + "></td></tr>");
        }
        // This statement outside the loop completes the table
        document.append("</table></td></tr></table>");
        //Calculate and display the monthly payment amount
        var monPmt = calcMonthly(loanAmount, numPay, intRate);
        // Call the amortization routine
        amortizePmts(loanAmount, intRate, numPay, monPmt);
        return;
    }

    function amortizePmts(loanAmount, intRate, numPay, monPmt) {
        var oldBalance = loanAmount;
        var newBalance = loanAmount;
        intRate = (intRate / 100) / 12;
        var monthly = monPmt;
        var owedInterest = 0;
        var totalInterestPd = 0;

        var tagNam;
        var dispInt
        // The for loop performs the amortization
        for (var i = 1; i <= numPay; i++) {
            var loopNum = i;
            owedInterest = newBalance * intRate;
            dispInt = twoDecimal(owedInterest);
            totalInterestPd = totalInterestPd + owedInterest;


            // Test for the final payment
//            if (i < numPay) {
                monthly = twoDecimal(monPmt - dispInt);
                oldBalance = newBalance;
                newBalance = twoDecimal(oldBalance - monthly);
//            }
//            else {
//                monthly = (oldBalance - monthly) + owedInterest;
//                oldBalance = newBalance;
//                newBalance = 0;
//                monthly = twoDecimal(monthly);
//            }

            var totalpayment = Math.round(monthly) + Math.round(dispInt);

            //tagNam = "b" + loopNum.toString(10);
            //displayTableField(tagNam, Math.round(oldBalance).toString().replace(/(\d)(?=(\d\d\d)+(?!\d))/g, "$1,"));
            tagNam = "p" + loopNum.toString(10);
            displayTableField(tagNam, Math.round(monthly).toString().replace(/(\d)(?=(\d\d\d)+(?!\d))/g, "$1,"));
            tagNam = "oi" + loopNum.toString(10);
            displayTableField(tagNam, Math.round(dispInt).toString().replace(/(\d)(?=(\d\d\d)+(?!\d))/g, "$1,"));
            tagNam = "ti" + loopNum.toString(10);
            displayTableField(tagNam, Math.round(totalpayment).toString().replace(/(\d)(?=(\d\d\d)+(?!\d))/g, "$1,"));
            tagNam = "nb" + loopNum.toString(10);
            displayTableField(tagNam, Math.round(newBalance).toString().replace(/(\d)(?=(\d\d\d)+(?!\d))/g, "$1,"));
        }
        return;
    }

    function displayTableField(eleId, eleDat) {
        document.getElementById(eleId).innerHTML = eleDat;
        return;
    }

    function calcMonthly(principal, numPay, intRate) {
        var monthly;
        var intRate = (intRate / 100) / 12;
        var principal;
        // The accounting formula to calculate the monthly payment is
        //    M = P * ((I + 1)^N) * I / (((I + 1)^N)-1)
        // The following code  transforms this accounting formula into JavaScript to calculate the monthly payment
        monthly = (principal * (Math.pow((1 + intRate), numPay)) * intRate / (Math.pow((1 + intRate), numPay) - 1));
        return twoDecimal(monthly);
    }

    function twoDecimal(chgVar) {
        var chgVar;
        var twoDec = chgVar.toFixed(2);
        return twoDec;
    }

</script>
